# TypeScript/Rust Organization Plan

This document is the review plan for reorganizing Marinara into a TypeScript domain engine backed by a small Rust capability kernel. It intentionally avoids exact implementation code. It inventories the current refactor repository and the original TypeScript source files so every file has an explicit home or disposition.

Scope notes: sidecar and sync-client are deferred external-service work and must not be part of the active runtime graph.

## Architecture Decision

Use TypeScript for expressive product behavior and Rust for privileged capabilities. The webview should not own secrets, arbitrary filesystem access, native process/device access, authenticated provider transport, or safe network policy. TypeScript should own agents, prompt rules, generation orchestration, chat/autonomous, game, and roleplay rules, and UI-facing application flow.

```text
React features
  -> shared/api adapters
  -> TypeScript engine use cases
      -> capability interfaces
          -> shared/api Tauri adapters
              -> Rust capability commands
```

## Non-Duplication Rules

- A behavior has one owner: React UI, TypeScript engine, or Rust capability.
- React components do not duplicate engine rules; they call hooks/use cases.
- TypeScript engine modules do not import React, Zustand stores, Tauri invoke, browser storage, or raw privileged fetch.
- Rust commands stay thin. They validate capability inputs, call Rust capability services, and return DTOs/events.
- Storage record shapes are defined once in TypeScript contracts for UI/engine and persisted through Rust storage adapters. Rust may validate capability inputs but should not reimplement product rules.
- Provider request construction may be TypeScript, but attaching secrets and making authenticated network calls is Rust.
- Do not add compatibility barrels, one-line re-export shims, or `legacy-shared` aliases. Import contracts and helpers from their owning files.

## Target Repository Shape

```text
src/
  app/                         React bootstrap, shell, providers, startup effects
  features/                    React feature UI, feature hooks, UI-only stores
  shared/
    api/                       Tauri-backed capability adapters
    components/                Shared React components
    hooks/                     Shared React/browser hooks
    lib/                       Browser/display helpers only
    stores/                    Ephemeral UI/session stores
    types/generated/           Optional generated Rust capability DTOs
  engine/                      React-free TypeScript domain engine
    core/
    contracts/
    capabilities/
    modes/
      chat/
      roleplay/
      game/
    prompt/
    lorebooks/
    regex/
    llm/
    generation/
    agents/
    integrations/
    imports/
src-tauri/
  src/                         Tauri host, state, commands, events
  crates/                      Rust capability crates
```

## Planned TypeScript Engine And API Files

| Planned file/module | Responsibility | Touches / dependencies |
| --- | --- | --- |
| src/engine/core/* | TS engine core primitives in owner files. | No React, no Tauri; avoid barrel-only files. |
| src/engine/core/result.ts | Small success/error helpers for engine use cases. | Shared by all engine modules. |
| src/engine/core/clock.ts | Clock abstraction for tests and scheduling. | Chat autonomous scheduling, agents, generation. |
| src/engine/core/ids.ts | Client-side temporary IDs where safe; durable IDs may come from Rust storage. | Chat draft UI, optimistic updates. |
| src/engine/contracts/* | TS-owned contracts imported from their owning files. | All TS modules; avoid a catch-all contracts barrel. |
| src/engine/contracts/constants/* | Copied shared constants. | UI and engine. |
| src/engine/contracts/types/* | Copied shared type contracts. | UI, engine, shared/api. |
| src/engine/contracts/schemas/* | Copied Zod schemas. | Form validation, command input validation. |
| src/engine/capabilities/storage.ts | Interface for durable entity reads/writes. | Implemented by shared/api Tauri adapter. |
| src/engine/capabilities/llm.ts | Interface for model calls, streaming, model discovery. | Implemented by Rust llm-transport adapter. |
| src/engine/capabilities/assets.ts | Interface for validated file/blob/media operations. | Implemented by Rust assets/imports commands. |
| src/engine/capabilities/integrations.ts | Interface for Spotify/TTS/translation/haptic/bot-browser operations. | Implemented by Rust integrations commands. |
| src/engine/capabilities/events.ts | Engine-facing event sink/source abstraction. | Backed by Tauri events. |
| src/engine/chat/service.ts | Chat domain operations above persistence: message metadata, swipes, branches, summaries. | StorageGateway only. |
| src/engine/chat/transcript.ts | Transcript normalization/sanitation. | Generation, conversation, roleplay. |
| src/engine/prompt/assembler.ts | Adapted prompt assembler with explicit input DTOs instead of DB. | Generation, game, prompt preview. |
| src/engine/prompt/macro-context.ts | Macro context builder. | Prompt, agents, game. |
| src/engine/prompt/format-engine.ts | Prompt wrapping/formatting. | Prompt assembler. |
| src/engine/prompt/marker-expander.ts | Preset marker expansion. | Prompt assembler. |
| src/engine/prompt/merger.ts | Message merge and squash helpers. | Prompt assembler, LLM context. |
| src/engine/lorebooks/keyword-scanner.ts | Lorebook keyword and condition matching. | Prompt/generation/game. |
| src/engine/lorebooks/prompt-injector.ts | Depth insertion into prompt messages. | Prompt assembler. |
| src/engine/lorebooks/service.ts | Lorebook scan orchestration over storage inputs. | StorageGateway, prompt. |
| src/engine/regex/regex-application.ts | Regex script application pipeline. | Generation, preview tools. |
| src/engine/llm/context-fit.ts | Context window fitting and token estimates. | Generation, agents. |
| src/engine/llm/messages.ts | Provider-neutral message/tool DTOs. | LlmGateway, agents, generation. |
| src/engine/generation/service.ts | Generation use case coordinator. | Prompt, lorebooks, regex, agents, chat, LlmGateway. |
| src/engine/generation/pipeline.ts | Preflight, prompt build, stream, postprocess, persistence steps. | Generation service. |
| src/engine/generation/events.ts | Typed generation event DTOs. | shared/api events. |
| src/engine/agents/agent-executor.ts | Adapted TS agent executor. | LlmGateway, tool router. |
| src/engine/agents/agent-pipeline.ts | Agent phase orchestration and batching. | Generation service. |
| src/engine/agents/agent-context.ts | Agent context builders and normalization. | Generation, chat. |
| src/engine/agents/agent-results.ts | Result parsing and normalization. | Agent executor. |
| src/engine/agents/knowledge-router.ts | Knowledge route decision logic. | StorageGateway, LlmGateway. |
| src/engine/agents/knowledge-retrieval.ts | Knowledge retrieval orchestration. | StorageGateway; embeddings via capability if retained. |
| src/engine/agents/tools/definitions.ts | Tool schemas exposed to LLMs. | Agent executor. |
| src/engine/agents/tools/pure-tools.ts | Dice, expression, metadata draft helpers. | No privileged IO. |
| src/engine/agents/tools/tool-router.ts | Routes tools to pure handlers or Rust capabilities. | IntegrationGateway, StorageGateway. |
| src/engine/modes/chat/autonomous/service.ts | Chat autonomous/conversation use cases. | Chat, generation, storage. |
| src/engine/modes/chat/schedules/schedule.ts | Schedule calculations. | Chat autonomous UI and scheduling. |
| src/engine/modes/chat/commands/commands.ts | Character/direct command parsing. | Generation and chat autonomous flows. |
| src/engine/modes/chat/summaries/summaries.ts | Summary backfill and formatting logic. | Chat metadata. |
| src/engine/roleplay/service.ts | Scene/sprite/encounter orchestration above storage. | Generation, assets capability. |
| src/engine/roleplay/scene.ts | Scene analysis request/response shaping. | LlmGateway or integration capability. |
| src/engine/roleplay/sprites.ts | Sprite metadata and placement rules. | Assets capability for files. |
| src/engine/game/mechanics/*.ts | Dice, checks, combat, loot, morale, reputation, perception, elements. | Game service. |
| src/engine/game/world/*.ts | Map, weather, time, journal, travel rules. | Game service, UI. |
| src/engine/game/prompts/*.ts | GM and party prompt builders. | Generation service. |
| src/engine/game/state/*.ts | Game state machine, snapshots, repair, checkpoints DTO logic. | StorageGateway. |
| src/engine/game/service.ts | Game turn orchestration above capabilities. | Generation, storage, assets. |
| src/engine/integrations/spotify/music-selection.ts | Playlist/music choice heuristics only. | Rust handles OAuth/playback. |
| src/engine/imports/review.ts | Import review normalization and conflict display helpers. | Rust handles filesystem scanning/reading. |
| src/shared/api/tauri-client.ts | Low-level typed invoke/listen wrapper. | All capability adapters. |
| src/shared/api/storage-api.ts | StorageGateway implementation over Tauri commands. | Engine services. |
| src/shared/api/llm-api.ts | LlmGateway implementation over Tauri commands/events. | Generation and agents. |
| src/shared/api/assets-api.ts | AssetsGateway implementation over Tauri commands. | UI and engine. |
| src/shared/api/integrations-api.ts | IntegrationGateway implementation over Tauri commands. | Tools and UI. |

## Planned Rust Capability Files

| Planned file/module | Responsibility |
| --- | --- |
| src-tauri/src/lib.rs | Tauri runtime entrypoint. Registers plugins, state, command groups, and event support; no domain logic. |
| src-tauri/src/main.rs | Binary entrypoint only. |
| src-tauri/src/app.rs | Builds Rust capability graph: config, storage, security, llm transport, assets, integrations, updates. |
| src-tauri/src/state.rs | Shared Arc handles passed into commands. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/mod.rs | Registers all command groups. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/storage.rs | CRUD/storage commands used by StorageGateway. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/llm.rs | Provider/model/streaming commands used by LlmGateway. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/assets.rs | Validated media/file/blob commands. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/imports.rs | Folder picker, ST scans, card import, profile import/export file access. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/integrations.rs | Spotify/TTS/translation/haptic/bot-browser commands. |
| src-tauri/src/commands/updates.rs | Update check/apply commands. |
| src-tauri/src/events/mod.rs | Typed event names and emit helpers. |
| src-tauri/crates/core/src/lib.rs | Rust error, paths, config, IDs, cancellation, logging foundations. |
| src-tauri/crates/security/src/lib.rs | Secrets, path safety, outbound URL policy, safe fetch, content type validation, permissions. |
| src-tauri/crates/storage/src/lib.rs | Raw file-backed storage manager, atomic writes, manifests, repositories, current Tauri migrations. |
| src-tauri/crates/llm/src/lib.rs | Authenticated provider transport, model discovery, streaming fetch, redaction, local URL policy. |
| src-tauri/crates/assets/src/lib.rs | Avatar/background/gallery/font/blob validation and placement. |
| src-tauri/crates/import/src/lib.rs | Filesystem import scanners, path tokens, PNG card IO, profile import/export file operations. |
| src-tauri/crates/integrations/src/lib.rs | OAuth, tokens, authenticated integration calls, native device calls. |
| src-tauri/crates/updates/src/lib.rs | Update metadata, permission-gated application. |

## Module Boundary Map

| Area | Owner | Touches | Reason |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Agents | TypeScript engine | Rust LLM transport, storage, integration tools, safe fetch for webhooks | Agent design remains accessible to TS developers; privileged execution is routed. |
| Generation | TypeScript engine | Rust LLM transport/events/storage | Prompt/pipeline rules stay TS; actual provider calls and event bridge are Rust-backed. |
| Chat | TypeScript engine above persistence | Rust storage capability | Swipes/branches/metadata semantics are TS; durable writes are Rust. |
| Prompt/Lorebook/Regex | TypeScript engine | Storage and optional embedding capabilities | Mostly copy/adapt existing TS. |
| Game | TypeScript engine | Rust storage/assets/LLM transport | Mechanics are not performance risky; keep in TS. |
| Chat autonomous/Roleplay | TypeScript engine | Rust storage/assets/LLM transport/integrations | Chat scheduling/autonomous rules and roleplay rules stay TS. |
| Storage | Rust capability | TypeScript StorageGateway | Atomic writes, manifests, and path safety need Rust. |
| Security | Rust capability | All adapters | Secrets, OAuth, cookies, safe fetch, path safety. |
| LLM provider calls | Rust transport with TS request shaping | Agents/generation | Secrets and SSRF policy stay Rust. |
| Integrations | Split | Rust auth/network/native; TS orchestration/heuristics | Spotify/TTS/translation/bot-browser/haptic. |
| Imports/assets | Split | Rust file access/validation; TS review UI/helpers | Keeps webview away from raw filesystem. |
| Sidecar | Deferred | None now | External-service scope. |
| Sync client | Deferred | None now | External-service scope. |

## Implementation Sequence

1. Add `src/engine` folders and capability interfaces without moving behavior yet.
2. Move shared contracts into `src/engine/contracts` owner files with direct imports; do not add temporary barrels or aliases.
3. Add `shared/api` Tauri adapter shells for storage, LLM, assets, imports, integrations, and events.
4. Implement Rust storage/security/LLM-transport foundations first because TS engine modules need those capabilities.
5. Copy/adapt prompt, lorebook, regex, and LLM context-fit helpers into `src/engine`.
6. Copy/adapt agents into `src/engine/agents` and split pure tools from capability tools.
7. Copy/adapt generation orchestration into `src/engine/generation`; switch streaming from SSE to Tauri events through `LlmGateway`.
8. Move game, conversation, and roleplay service logic into `src/engine`, replacing DB/filesystem/network calls with gateways.
9. Update React hooks to call engine use cases and shared/api adapters.
10. Remove old `/api` seams, placeholder unavailable calls, and any compatibility shims after each vertical slice is real.

## Review Questions

- Should TypeScript contracts be the long-term source of truth, or should Rust generate only capability DTOs while engine DTOs remain TS-owned?
- Which custom tool types should be allowed in desktop: static only, webhook through Rust safe fetch, or sandboxed scripts?
- Should provider-specific request body construction remain TS, or should Rust own each provider format once transport moves?
- Do we want the engine to run only in the webview, or eventually in a separate JS worker/runtime for isolation?
- Which sidecar and sync files should be removed from near-term docs versus kept as placeholders?
